This code is based on accneat. Although some small changes 
have been made, most of the NEAT algorithm remains unchanged.

Accneat is a fork of Stanley et al.'s implementation with some 
improvements such as delete mutations and speed improvements, available at 
https://github.com/sean-dougherty/accneat


This code also uses a configuration file parser inih, available at https://github.com/jtilly/inih
The authors of the modified software distributed here are in NO way affiliated with accneat or INIH. Please, 
understand that the use of this software requires reading and accepting the licences of both accneat and INIH.

INIH is distributed with BSD licence, and accneat with APACHE LICENCE 2.0
The source code provided here (excluding accneat and INIH) was made by Etor Arza.
To keep the licence stuff as painless as possible, the software part writen by 
Etor Arza is distributed with APACHE LICENCE 2.0 too.
